I am posting the directions in my review and as long as you are following the simple directions, this does remove the hair it advertises it will. I also didn't mind the smell of the cream as it is very mild but does the job.<br /><br />Lightly apply the Skin Guard Balm across the middle of the areas you wish to treat. Be sure the layer is thin, and apply it only once for effective hair removal. Massage Skin Guarding Balm Use your fingers to massage the balm into your skin, going beyond the area you wish to treat. Massage for 20 seconds in a circular motion. This ensures there is a pre-treatment layer to keep the Hair Removal Cream from coming in direct contact with your skin, and that hairs aren't overly coated. 2 REMOVE THE HAIR Apply Hair Removal Cream Apply a layer of Hair Removal Cream to your fingertip (small grape size for upper lip treatment) and immediately smooth over the area to be treated. For the product to work effectively, cover the skin completely with a thick layer but do not rub it in. Use only with the Skin Guarding Balm provided. Wash hands immediately and thoroughly. Let process for 6-8 minutes. Leave on longer for thicker hair, but do not exceed 10 minutes. Remove Hair / Cream After 6-8 minutes, gently remove cream with a tissue or cotton ball. Rinse your skin thoroughly with lukewarm water and pat dry.<br /><br />All in all, simple, AND effective...
